CREATE TABLE `copart_csv_sale` (
  `lot_number` bigint NOT NULL,
  `announcements` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `auto_grade` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `body_style` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `buy_it_now_price` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `color` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `copart_select` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `create_date_time` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `currency_code` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `cylinders` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `damage_description` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `day_of_week` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `drive` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `engine` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `est_retail_value` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `fuel_type` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `grid_row` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `has_keys` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `high_bid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `image_thumbnail` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `imageurl` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `item_number` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_updated_time` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `location_city` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `location_country` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `location_state` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `location_zip` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `lot_cond_code` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `make` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `make_an_offer_eligible` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `model_detail` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `model_group` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `odometer` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `odometer_brand` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `offsite_address1` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `offsite_city` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `offsite_state` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `offsite_zip` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `rentals` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `repair_cost` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `runs_drives` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sale_date` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sale_light` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sale_status` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sale_time` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sale_title_state` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sale_title_type` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `secondary_damage` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `seller_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `special_note` varchar(1024) DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_zone` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `transmission` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `trim` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `vehicle_type` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `vin` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `yard_number` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `year` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_update_created` datetime(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `yard_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `wholesale` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`lot_number`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;

CREATE TABLE `copart_images` (
  `url` varchar(512) NOT NULL,
  `is_hd_image` bit(1) NOT NULL,
  `is_thumb_nail` bit(1) NOT NULL,
  `lot_number` bigint NOT NULL,
  `sequence` int NOT NULL,
  `urls3` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_need_delete` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`url`),
  KEY `lot_number` (`lot_number`),
  KEY `ii` (`is_hd_image`,`is_thumb_nail`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci;
